NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICES
PUBLIC NOTICE

We, M/s, Ajit Kumar and Dilip Kumar, Partners of M/s. Arya Bhavan, No. 135, Govindappa Street, Chennai-600 001,
have dissolved our Partnership with M/s. R. Raman, R. Ramakrishna, G.N. Subbarayalu, R. Venkatesh and R. Shankar
vide Notice, dated 18th September 2009. The Leasehold Rights and Hotel Licence Belong to us Exclusively. No other person
is entitled to carry on business at the Aforesaid Premises. Any person Dealing with Anyone other than us shall do so at their
own risk.
Chennai,
4th June 2010.

AJIT KUMAR,
DILIP KUMAR,
Partners.

FORM No. 155
(See-Rule 329)
MEMBER’S VOLUNTARY WINDING UP
Notice of Teletech Investments (India) Limited
Notice convening Final Meeting

Notice is hereby given in pursuance of provisions of Section 497, that a General Meeting of the members of the above
named Company will be held at 56, New No. 77, C.P. Ramaswamy Road, Abhiramapuram, Chennai-600 018 on Thursday,
the 15th day of July, 2010 at 5.00 P.M. for the purpose of having an account laid before them showing the manner in which
the winding-up has been conducted and the property of the Company disposed of and of hearing any explanation that may
be given by the Liquidator and also of determining by a special resolution of the Company, the manner in which the books,
accounts and documents of the Company and of the Liquidator shall be disposed of.
Dated the 24th day of May 2010.
Chennai,
4th June 2010.

T.N.V. VISWESWARA RAO,
Liquidator.
